The program is daily filled with recipes from our customers and contains recipes for all occasions.\r\n\r\nAll recipes have a uniform style, which simplifies the understanding of the method of cooking.\r\n\r\nEach recipe has a description, list of ingredients, difficulty level, category food, cooking method, cooking time and calories. Also an author of dishes, as well as comments from the author and rating of dishes.\r\n\r\nThe most important part of the program is the obligatory presence of photos of a finished dish, as well as its cooking steps. Each step of cooking has a number of steps, photo, used in this step ingredients and description.\r\n\r\nFor your convenience, the size of a displayed recipe steps can be set by a user. Thus, all the steps of a recipe can be displayed on a screen at once. Also, each recipe can be opened in a separate window.\r\n\r\nIt is possible in the program to search recipes on the set parameters (category food, cooking method, cooking time, number of calories, title, chosen product). An important feature is the ability to search recipes by the products You have!\r\n\r\nWrite your own recipes. Thus, Your recipe will appear in a category of new recipes and will be visible to every user of the program. You will be specified as the author of the recipe.
